# rocSOLVER LAPACK auxiliary functions[#](#rocsolver-lapack-auxiliary-functions)

These are functions that support more [advanced LAPACK routines](lapack.html#lapackfunc).
The auxiliary functions are divided into the following categories:

[Vector and matrix manipulations](#vecmat): Basic operations with vectors and matrices that are not part of the BLAS standard.[Householder reflections](#householder): Generation and application of Householder matrices.[Givens (plane) rotations](#rotations): Generation and application of Givens (plane) rotations.[Bidiagonal forms](#bidiag): Computations specialized in bidiagonal matrices.[Tridiagonal forms](#tridiag): Computations specialized in tridiagonal matrices.[Symmetric matrices](#symmetric): Computations specialized in symmetric matrices.[Orthonormal matrices](#orthonormal): Generation and application of orthonormal matrices.[Unitary matrices](#unitary): Generation and application of unitary matrices.

Note

The API descriptions use the following notations:

`i`

,`j`

, and`k`

are used as general purpose indices. In some legacy LAPACK APIs,`k`

can be a parameter indicating some problem or matrix dimension.Depending on the context, when it is necessary to index rows, columns, and blocks or submatrices,

`i`

is assigned to rows,`j`

to columns, and`k`

to blocks.`l`

is always used to index matrices or problems in a batch.`x[i]`

stands for the i-th element of vector x, while`A[i,j]`

represents the element in the i-th row and j-th column of matrix`A`

. Indices are 1-based, for instance,`x[1]`

is the first element of`x`

.To identify a block in a matrix or a matrix in the batch,

`k`

and`l`

are used as sub-indices`x_i`

\(=x_i\). Both notations are used, \(x_i\) when displaying mathematical equations and`x_i`

in the text describing the function parameters.If

`X`

is a real vector or matrix, \(X^T\) indicates its transpose. If`X`

is complex, then \(X^H\) represents its conjugate transpose. When`X`

could be real or complex, the descriptions use`X'`

to indicate`X`

transposed or`X`

conjugate transposed, accordingly.When a matrix

`A`

is formed as the product of several matrices, the following notation is used:`A=M(1)M(2)...M(t)`

.

## Vector and matrix manipulations[#](#vector-and-matrix-manipulations)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlacgv([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlacgv14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clacgv([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clacgv14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) LACGV conjugates the complex vector x.

It conjugates the n entries of a complex vector x with increment incx.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The dimension of vector x.**x**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size at least n (size depends on the value of incx). On entry, the vector x. On exit, each entry is overwritten with its conjugate value.**incx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incx != 0. The distance between two consecutive elements of x. If incx is negative, the elements of x are indexed in reverse order.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlaswp([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k1, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k2, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlaswp14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_claswp([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k1, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k2, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_claswp14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlaswp([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k1, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k2, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlaswp14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slaswp([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k1, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k2, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slaswp14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) LASWP performs a series of row interchanges on the matrix A.

Row interchanges are done one by one. If \(\text{ipiv}[k_1 + (j - k_1) \cdot \text{abs}(\text{incx})] = r\), then the j-th row of A will be interchanged with the r-th row of A, for \(j = k_1,k_1+1,\dots,k_2\). Indices \(k_1\) and \(k_2\) are 1-based indices.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix to which the row interchanges will be applied. On exit, the resulting permuted matrix.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda > 0. The leading dimension of the array A.**k1**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k1 > 0. The k_1 index. It is the first element of ipiv for which a row interchange will be done. This is a 1-based index.**k2**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k2 > k1 > 0. The k_2 index. k_2 - k_1 + 1 is the number of elements of ipiv for which a row interchange will be done. This is a 1-based index.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension at least \(k_1 + (k_2 - k_1)\cdot \text{abs}(\text{incx})\). The vector of pivot indices. Only the elements in positions \(k_1\) through \(k_1 + (k_2 - k_1)\cdot \text{abs}(\text{incx})\) of this vector are accessed. Elements of ipiv are considered 1-based.**incx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incx != 0. The distance between successive values of ipiv. If incx is negative, the pivots are applied in reverse order.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlauum([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlauum14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clauum([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clauum14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlauum([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlauum14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slauum([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slauum14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_int) LAUUM computes the product of the upper (or lower) triangular part U (or L) of a symmetric/Hemitian matrix A with its transpose.

If uplo indicates upper, then \(UU'\) is computed. If uplo indicates lower, then \(L'L\) is computed instead.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower triangular part of A will be used. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not referenced.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns and rows of the matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, it contains the upper (or lower) part of the symmetric/Hermitian matrix. On exit, the upper (or lower) part is overwritten with the result of U*U’ (or L’*L).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. The leading dimension of the array A.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clarfg([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*alpha,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*tau)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clarfg14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlarfg([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *alpha, double *x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, double *tau)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlarfg14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_intPd)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slarfg([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *alpha, float *x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, float *tau)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slarfg14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_intPf) LARFG generates a Householder reflector H of order n.

The reflector H is such that

\[\begin{split} H'\left[\begin{array}{c} \text{alpha}\\ x \end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c} \text{beta}\\ 0 \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]where x is an n-1 vector, and alpha and beta are scalars. Matrix H can be generated as

\[\begin{split} H = I - \text{tau}\left[\begin{array}{c} 1\\ v \end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{cc} 1 & v' \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]where v is an n-1 vector, and tau is a scalar known as the Householder scalar. The vector

\[\begin{split} \bar{v}=\left[\begin{array}{c} 1\\ v \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]is the Householder vector associated with the reflection.

Note

The matrix H is orthogonal/unitary (i.e. \(H'H=HH'=I\)). It is symmetric when real (i.e. \(H^T=H\)), but not Hermitian when complex (i.e. \(H^H\neq H\) in general).

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The order (size) of reflector H.**alpha**–**[inout]**pointer to type. A scalar on the GPU. On entry, the scalar alpha. On exit, it is overwritten with beta.**x**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size at least n-1 (size depends on the value of incx). On entry, the vector x, On exit, it is overwritten with vector v.**incx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incx > 0. The distance between two consecutive elements of x.**tau**–**[out]**pointer to type. A scalar on the GPU. The Householder scalar tau.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlarft([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*tau,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlarft14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clarft([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*tau,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clarft14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlarft([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, double *tau, double *T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlarft14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slarft([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, float *tau, float *T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slarft14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) LARFT generates the triangular factor T of a block reflector H of order n.

The block reflector H is defined as the product of k Householder matrices

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} H = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) & \: \text{if direct indicates forward direction, or} \\ H = H(k)\cdots H(2)H(1) & \: \text{if direct indicates backward direction} \end{array} \end{split}\]The triangular factor T is upper triangular in the forward direction and lower triangular in the backward direction. If storev is column-wise, then

\[ H = I - VTV' \]where the \(j\)th column of matrix V contains the Householder vector associated with \(H(j)\). If storev is row-wise, then

\[ H = I - V'TV \]where the \(i\)th row of matrix V contains the Householder vector associated with \(H(i)\).

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**direct**–**[in]**[rocblas_direct](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a8cb9be11d12e3c9eb2b8f707888a8482). Specifies the direction in which the Householder matrices are applied.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies how the Householder vectors are stored in matrix V.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The order (size) of the block reflector.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 1. The number of Householder matrices forming H.**V**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldv*k if column-wise, or ldv*n if row-wise. The matrix of Householder vectors.**ldv**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldv >= n if column-wise, or ldv >= k if row-wise. Leading dimension of V.**tau**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array of k scalars on the GPU. The vector of all the Householder scalars.**T**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldt*k. The triangular factor. T is upper triangular if direct indicates forward direction, otherwise it is lower triangular. The rest of the array is not used.**ldt**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldt >= k. The leading dimension of T.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlarf_64([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const int64_t m, const int64_t n, double *x, const int64_t incx, const double *alpha, double *A, const int64_t lda)[#](#_CPPv418rocsolver_dlarf_6414rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK7int64_tK7int64_tPdK7int64_tPKdPdK7int64_t)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlarf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*alpha,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_zlarf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intPK22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clarf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*alpha,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_clarf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intPK21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlarf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const double *alpha, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_dlarf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPKdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slarf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *x, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const float *alpha, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_slarf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPKfPfK11rocblas_int) LARF applies a Householder reflector H to a general matrix A.

The Householder reflector H, of order m or n, is to be applied to an m-by-n matrix A from the left or the right, depending on the value of side. H is given by

\[ H = I - \text{alpha}\cdot xx' \]where alpha is the Householder scalar and x is a Householder vector. H is never actually computed.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Determines whether H is applied from the left or the right.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of A.**x**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size at least 1 + (m-1)*abs(incx) if left side, or at least 1 + (n-1)*abs(incx) if right side. The Householder vector x.**incx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incx != 0. Distance between two consecutive elements of x. If incx < 0, the elements of x are indexed in reverse order.**alpha**–**[in]**pointer to type. A scalar on the GPU. The Householder scalar. If alpha = 0, then H = I (A will remain the same; x is never used)**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, it is overwritten with H*A (or A*H).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Leading dimension of A.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlarfb([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlarfb([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, double *T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlarfb14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slarfb([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, float *T, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldt, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slarfb14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK14rocblas_directK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_int) LARFB applies a block reflector H to a general m-by-n matrix A.

The block reflector H is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} HA & \: \text{(No transpose from the left),}\\ H'A & \: \text{(Transpose or conjugate transpose from the left),}\\ AH & \: \text{(No transpose from the right), or}\\ AH' & \: \text{(Transpose or conjugate transpose from the right).} \end{array} \end{split}\]The block reflector H is defined as the product of k Householder matrices as

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} H = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) & \: \text{if direct indicates forward direction, or} \\ H = H(k)\cdots H(2)H(1) & \: \text{if direct indicates backward direction} \end{array} \end{split}\]H is never stored. It is calculated as

\[ H = I - VTV' \]where the \(j\)th column of matrix V contains the Householder vector associated with \(H(j)\), if storev is column-wise; or

\[ H = I - V'TV \]where the \(i\)th row of matrix V contains the Householder vector associated with \(H(i)\), if storev is row-wise. T is the associated triangular factor as computed by

[LARFT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a752e5fe40282cfc92e61d0c6a233b191).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply H.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the block reflector or its transpose/conjugate transpose is to be applied.**direct**–**[in]**[rocblas_direct](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a8cb9be11d12e3c9eb2b8f707888a8482). Specifies the direction in which the Householder matrices are to be applied to generate H.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies how the Householder vectors are stored in matrix V.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix A.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 1. The number of Householder matrices.**V**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldv*k if column-wise, ldv*n if row-wise and applying from the right, or ldv*m if row-wise and applying from the left. The matrix of Householder vectors.**ldv**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldv >= k if row-wise, ldv >= m if column-wise and applying from the left, or ldv >= n if column-wise and applying from the right. Leading dimension of V.**T**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldt*k. The triangular factor of the block reflector.**ldt**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldt >= k. The leading dimension of T.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, it is overwritten with H*A, A*H, H’*A, or A*H’.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Leading dimension of A.



## Givens (plane) rotations[#](#givens-plane-rotations)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlasr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_pivot](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_pivot)pivot, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *C, double *S,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_zlasr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK13rocblas_pivotK14rocblas_directK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdPdP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clasr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_pivot](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_pivot)pivot, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *C, float *S,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_clasr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK13rocblas_pivotK14rocblas_directK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfPfP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlasr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_pivot](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_pivot)pivot, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *C, double *S, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_dlasr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK13rocblas_pivotK14rocblas_directK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slasr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_pivot](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_pivot)pivot, const[rocblas_direct](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_direct)direct, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *C, float *S, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda)[#](#_CPPv415rocsolver_slasr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK13rocblas_pivotK14rocblas_directK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfPfPfK11rocblas_int) LASR applies a sequence of Givens plane rotations, represented as a transformation P, to a general m-by-n matrix A.

The transformation P is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the value of side:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} PA & \: \text{(No transpose from the left),}\\ AP^T & \: \text{(Transpose from the right).} \end{array} \end{split}\]P is defined as the product of k plane rotations, with k = m - 1 when applied from the left, and k = n - 1 when applied from the right, as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} P = P(1)P(2)\cdots P(k) & \: \text{if direct indicates backward direction, or} \\ P = P(k)\cdots P(2)P(1) & \: \text{if direct indicates forward direction} \end{array} \end{split}\]Each P(i) is defined by a Givens rotation

\[\begin{split} R(i) = \left[\begin{array}{cc} c_i & s_i \\ -s_i & c_i \end{array}\right], \end{split}\]where the \(c_i\) and \(s_i\) are the corresponding cosine and sine factors.

The rotations are performed on different planes depending on the value of pivot. If pivot is variable, the rotation R(i) is performed on plane (i,i+1), i.e. P(i) appears as a rank-2 modification to the identity matrix in the i-th and (i+1)-th rows and columns. If pivot is top, then the modification appears in the first and (i+1)-th rows and columns of P(i), and if pivot is bottom, then the modification appears in the i-th and last rows and columns of P(i).

All rotations are applied directly without ever forming P(i) explicitly.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply P.**pivot**–**[in]**[rocblas_pivot](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1aec4a87196ea90f89ca9608ac9543bd7f). Specifies the planes on which the rotations are applied.**direct**–**[in]**[rocblas_direct](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a8cb9be11d12e3c9eb2b8f707888a8482). Specifies the direction in which the plane rotations are to be applied to generate P.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix A.**C**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of size n-1 if side is right, or m-1 if side is left. Contains the series of cosine factors defining the Givens rotations.**S**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of size n-1 if side is right, or m-1 if side is left. Contains the series of sine factors defining the Givens rotations.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, it is overwritten with P*A, or A*P^T.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Leading dimension of A.



## Bidiagonal forms[#](#bidiagonal-forms)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlabrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *D, double *E,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*tauq,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*taup,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*Y, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldy)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlabrd14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intPdPdP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clabrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*tauq,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*taup,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*Y, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldy)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clabrd14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intPfPfP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlabrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *D, double *E, double *tauq, double *taup, double *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, double *Y, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldy)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlabrd14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdPdPdPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slabrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *D, float *E, float *tauq, float *taup, float *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, float *Y, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldy)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slabrd14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfPfPfPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_int) LABRD computes the bidiagonal form of the first k rows and columns of a general m-by-n matrix A, as well as the matrices X and Y needed to reduce the remaining part of A.

The reduced form is given by:

\[ B = Q'AP \]where the leading k-by-k block of B is upper bidiagonal if m >= n, or lower bidiagonal if m < n. Q and P are orthogonal/unitary matrices represented as the product of Householder matrices

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k), & \text{and} \\ P = G(1)G(2)\cdots G(k). \end{array} \end{split}\]Each Householder matrix \(H(i)\) and \(G(i)\) is given by

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} H(i) = I - \text{tauq}[i]\cdot v_i^{}v_i', & \text{and} \\ G(i) = I - \text{taup}[i]\cdot u_i^{}u_i'. \end{array} \end{split}\]If m >= n, the first \(i-1\) elements of the Householder vector \(v_i\) are zero, and \(v_i[i]=1\); while the first \(i\) elements of the Householder vector \(u_i\) are zero, and \(u_i[i+1]=1\). If m < n, the first \(i\) elements of the Householder vector \(v_i\) are zero, and \(v_i[i+1]=1\); while the first \(i-1\) elements of the Householder vector \(u_i\) are zero, and \(u_i[i]=1\).

The unreduced part of the matrix A can be updated using the block update

\[ A = A - VY' - XU' \]where V and U are the m-by-k and n-by-k matrices formed with the vectors \(v_i\) and \(u_i\), respectively.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix A.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. min(m,n) >= k >= 0. The number of leading rows and columns of matrix A that will be reduced.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the m-by-n matrix to be reduced. On exit, the first k elements on the diagonal and superdiagonal (if m >= n), or subdiagonal (if m < n), contain the bidiagonal form B. If m >= n, the elements below the diagonal of the first k columns are the possibly non-zero elements of the Householder vectors associated with Q, while the elements above the superdiagonal of the first k rows are the n - i - 1 possibly non-zero elements of the Householder vectors related to P. If m < n, the elements below the subdiagonal of the first k columns are the m - i - 1 possibly non-zero elements of the Householder vectors related to Q, while the elements above the diagonal of the first k rows are the n - i possibly non-zero elements of the vectors associated with P.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**D**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension k. The diagonal elements of B.**E**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension k. The off-diagonal elements of B.**tauq**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension k. The Householder scalars associated with matrix Q.**taup**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension k. The Householder scalars associated with matrix P.**X**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldx*k. The m-by-k matrix needed to update the unreduced part of A.**ldx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldx >= m. The leading dimension of X.**Y**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldy*k. The n-by-k matrix needed to update the unreduced part of A.**ldy**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldy >= n. The leading dimension of Y.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dbdsqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nc, double *D, double *E, double *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, double *U, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldu, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dbdsqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdPdPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sbdsqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nv, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nc, float *D, float *E, float *V, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldv, float *U, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldu, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sbdsqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfPfPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) BDSQR computes the singular value decomposition (SVD) of an n-by-n bidiagonal matrix B, using the implicit QR algorithm.

The SVD of B has the form:

\[ B = QSP' \]where S is the n-by-n diagonal matrix of singular values of B, the columns of Q are the left singular vectors of B, and the columns of P are its right singular vectors.

The computation of the singular vectors is optional; this function accepts input matrices U (of size nu-by-n) and V (of size n-by-nv) that are overwritten with \(UQ\) and \(P'V\). If nu = 0 no left vectors are computed; if nv = 0 no right vectors are computed.

Optionally, this function can also compute \(Q'C\) for a given n-by-nc input matrix C.

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

Note

A hybrid (CPU+GPU) approach is available for BDSQR, primarily intended for homogeneous architectures. Use

[rocsolver_set_alg_mode](helpers.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad95bfd9a74e1d41579facf7f305ed78c)to enable it.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether B is upper or lower bidiagonal.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of matrix B.**nv**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nv >= 0. The number of columns of matrix V.**nu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nu >= 0. The number of rows of matrix U.**nc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nc >= 0. The number of columns of matrix C.**D**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On entry, the diagonal elements of B. On exit, if info = 0, the singular values of B in decreasing order; if info > 0, the diagonal elements of a bidiagonal matrix orthogonally equivalent to B.**E**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. On entry, the off-diagonal elements of B. On exit, if info > 0, the off-diagonal elements of a bidiagonal matrix orthogonally equivalent to B (if info = 0 this matrix converges to zero).**V**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldv*nv. On entry, the matrix V. On exit, it is overwritten with P’*V. (Not referenced if nv = 0).**ldv**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldv >= n if nv > 0, or ldv >=1 if nv = 0. The leading dimension of V.**U**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldu*n. On entry, the matrix U. On exit, it is overwritten with U*Q. (Not referenced if nu = 0).**ldu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldu >= nu. The leading dimension of U.**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*nc. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q’*C. (Not referenced if nc = 0).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n if nc > 0, or ldc >=1 if nc = 0. The leading dimension of C.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, i elements of E have not converged to zero.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dbdsvdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_svect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_svect)svect, const[rocblas_srange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_srange)srange, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nsv, double *S, double *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_dbdsvdx14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK13rocblas_svectK14rocblas_srangeK11rocblas_intPdPdKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sbdsvdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_svect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_svect)svect, const[rocblas_srange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_srange)srange, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nsv, float *S, float *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_sbdsvdx14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK13rocblas_svectK14rocblas_srangeK11rocblas_intPfPfKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) BDSVDX computes a set of singular values of a bidiagonal matrix B.

This function computes all the singular values of B, all the singular values in the half-open interval \([vl, vu)\), or the il-th through iu-th singular values, depending on the value of srange.

Depending on the value of svect, the corresponding singular vectors will be computed and stored as blocks in the output matrix Z. That is,

\[\begin{split} Z = \left[\begin{array}{c} U\\ V \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]where U contains the corresponding left singular vectors of B, and V contains the corresponding right singular vectors.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether B is upper or lower bidiagonal.**svect**–**[in]**[rocblas_svect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a5959bd5c6a89fc7ec890cf5f35108893). Specifies how the singular vectors are computed. Only rocblas_svect_none and rocblas_svect_singular are accepted.**srange**–**[in]**[rocblas_srange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a0e8dea882e55c1dea5a7a107a0bf1f6a). Specifies the type of range or interval of the singular values to be computed.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The order of the bidiagonal matrix B.**D**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The diagonal elements of the bidiagonal matrix.**E**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. The off-diagonal elements of the bidiagonal matrix.**vl**–**[in]**real type. 0 <= vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval [vl, vu). Ignored if srange indicates to look for all the singular values of B or the singular values within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. 0 <= vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval [vl, vu). Ignored if srange indicates to look for all the singular values of B or the singular values within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the largest singular value to be computed. Ignored if srange indicates to look for all the singular values of B or the singular values in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest singular value to be computed. Ignored if srange indicates to look for all the singular values of B or the singular values in a half-open interval.**nsv**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of singular values found. If srange is rocblas_srange_all, nsv = n. If srange is rocblas_srange_index, nsv = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nsv <= n.**S**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension nsv. The first nsv elements contain the computed singular values in descending order. Note: If srange is rocblas_srange_value, then the value of nsv is not known in advance. In this case, the user should ensure that S is large enough to hold n values.**Z**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nsv. If info = 0, the first nsv columns contain the computed singular vectors corresponding to the singular values in S. The first n rows of Z contain the matrix U, and the next n rows contain the matrix V. Not referenced if svect is rocblas_svect_none. Note: If srange is rocblas_srange_value, then the value of nsv is not known in advance. In this case, the user should ensure that Z is large enough to hold n columns.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= 2*n if svect is rocblas_svect_singular; ldz >= 1 otherwise. Specifies the leading dimension of Z.**ifail**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. If info = 0, the first nsv elements of ifail are zero. Otherwise, contains the indices of those eigenvectors that failed to converge, as returned by[STEIN](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a459de4818d1dc67ffb18fd419d270ba7). Not referenced if svect is rocblas_svect_none.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, i eigenvectors did not converge in[STEIN](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a459de4818d1dc67ffb18fd419d270ba7); their indices are stored in ifail.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clatrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *E,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*tau,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*W, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldw)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clatrd14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intPfP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int)
