[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlatrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *E, double *tau, double *W, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldw)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlatrd14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slatrd([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *E, float *tau, float *W, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldw)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slatrd14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfPfK11rocblas_int) LATRD computes the tridiagonal form of k rows and columns of a symmetric/hermitian matrix A, as well as the matrix W needed to update the remaining part of A.

The reduced form is given by:

\[ T = Q'AQ \]If uplo is lower, the first k rows and columns of T form the tridiagonal block. If uplo is upper, then the last k rows and columns of T form the tridiagonal block. Q is an orthogonal/unitary matrix represented as the product of Householder matrices

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) & \text{if uplo indicates lower, or}\\ Q = H(n)H(n-1)\cdots H(n-k+1) & \text{if uplo is upper}. \end{array} \end{split}\]Each Householder matrix \(H(i)\) is given by

\[ H(i) = I - \text{tau}[i]\cdot v_i^{}v_i' \]where tau[ \(i\)] is the corresponding Householder scalar. When uplo indicates lower, the first \(i\) elements of the Householder vector \(v_i\) are zero, and \(v_i[i+1] = 1\). If uplo is upper, the last n- \(i\) elements of the Householder vector \(v_i\) are zero, and \(v_i[i] = 1\).

The unreduced part of the matrix A can be updated using a rank update of the form:

\[ A = A - VW' - WV' \]where V is the n-by-k matrix formed by the vectors \(v_i\).

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A to be reduced.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the n-by-n matrix to be reduced. On exit, if uplo is lower, the first k columns have been reduced to tridiagonal form (given in the diagonal elements of A and the array E), the elements below the diagonal contain the possibly non-zero entries of the Householder vectors associated with Q, stored as columns. If uplo is upper, the last k columns have been reduced to tridiagonal form (given in the diagonal elements of A and the array E), the elements above the diagonal contain the possibly non-zero entries of the Householder vectors associated with Q, stored as columns.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. The leading dimension of A.**E**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. If upper (lower), the last (first) k elements of E are the off-diagonal elements of the computed tridiagonal block.**tau**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. If upper (lower), the last (first) k elements of tau are the Householder scalars related to Q.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldw*k. The n-by-k matrix needed to update the unreduced part of A.**ldw**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldw >= n. The leading dimension of W.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsterf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dsterf14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdPdP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssterf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_ssterf14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfPfP11rocblas_int) STERF computes the eigenvalues of a symmetric tridiagonal matrix.

The eigenvalues of the symmetric tridiagonal matrix are computed by the Pal-Walker-Kahan variant of the QL/QR algorithm, and returned in increasing order.

The matrix is not represented explicitly, but rather as the array of diagonal elements D and the array of symmetric off-diagonal elements E.

Note

A hybrid (CPU+GPU) approach is available for STERF, primarily intended for homogeneous architectures. Use

[rocsolver_set_alg_mode](helpers.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad95bfd9a74e1d41579facf7f305ed78c)to enable it.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the tridiagonal matrix.**D**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On entry, the diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, the eigenvalues in increasing order. If info > 0, the diagonal elements of a tridiagonal matrix that is similar to the original matrix (i.e. has the same eigenvalues).**E**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. On entry, the off-diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, this array converges to zero. If info > 0, the off-diagonal elements of a tridiagonal matrix that is similar to the original matrix (i.e. has the same eigenvalues).**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, STERF did not converge. i elements of E did not converge to zero.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dstebz([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_eorder](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_eorder)eorder, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu, const double abstol, double *D, double *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nsplit, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dstebz14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_erangeK14rocblas_eorderK11rocblas_intKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intKdPdPdP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sstebz([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_eorder](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_eorder)eorder, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu, const float abstol, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nsplit, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sstebz14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_erangeK14rocblas_eorderK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intKfPfPfP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) STEBZ computes a set of eigenvalues of a symmetric tridiagonal matrix T.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of T, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval (vl, vu], or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange.

The eigenvalues are returned in increasing order either for the entire matrix, or grouped by independent diagonal blocks (if they exist), depending on the value of eorder.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**eorder**–**[in]**[rocblas_eorder](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a37fdea38babb4ebda6327c0b76e342aa). Specifies whether the computed eigenvalues will be ordered by their position in the entire spectrum, or grouped by independent diagonal (split off) blocks.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The order of the tridiagonal matrix T.**vl**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if erange indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of T or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if erange indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of T or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if erange indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of T or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if erange indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of T or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. An eigenvalue is considered to be located if it lies in an interval whose width is <= abstol. If abstol is negative, then machine-epsilon times the 1-norm of the tridiagonal form of A will be used as tolerance. If abstol=0, then the tolerance will be set to twice the underflow threshold; this is the tolerance that could get the most accurate results.**D**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix.**E**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. The off-diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found.**nsplit**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The number of split off blocks in the matrix.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The first nev elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**iblock**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The block indices corresponding to each eigenvalue. When matrix T has split off blocks (nsplit > 1), then if iblock[i] = k, the eigenvalue W[i] belongs to the k-th diagonal block from the top.**isplit**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The splitting indices that divide the tridiagonal matrix into diagonal blocks. The k-th block stretches from the end of the (k-1)-th block (or the top left corner of the tridiagonal matrix, in the case of the 1st block) to the isplit[k]-th row/column.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the bisection did not converge for some eigenvalues, i.e. the returned values are not as accurate as the given tolerance. The non-converged eigenvalues are flagged by negative entries in iblock.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_csteqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_csteqr14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPfPfP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsteqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dsteqr14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPdPdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssteqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_ssteqr14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPfPfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) STEQR computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a symmetric tridiagonal matrix.

The eigenvalues of the symmetric tridiagonal matrix are computed by the implicit QL/QR algorithm, and returned in increasing order.

The matrix is not represented explicitly, but rather as the array of diagonal elements D and the array of symmetric off-diagonal elements E. When D and E correspond to the tridiagonal form of a full symmetric/Hermitian matrix, as returned by, e.g.,

[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)or[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35), the eigenvectors of the original matrix can also be computed, depending on the value of evect.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies how the eigenvectors are computed.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the tridiagonal matrix.**D**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On entry, the diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, the eigenvalues in increasing order. If info > 0, the diagonal elements of a tridiagonal matrix that is similar to the original matrix (i.e. has the same eigenvalues).**E**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. On entry, the off-diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, this array converges to zero. If info > 0, the off-diagonal elements of a tridiagonal matrix that is similar to the original matrix (i.e. has the same eigenvalues).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. On entry, if evect is original, the orthogonal/unitary matrix used for the reduction to tridiagonal form as returned by, e.g.,[ORGTR](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1acaa6f0e82b62cf3aee9522e09dcc421e)or[UNGTR](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a31b4297ed23d32e373c67858ab89fa23). On exit, it is overwritten with the eigenvectors of the original symmetric/Hermitian matrix (if evect is original), or the eigenvectors of the tridiagonal matrix (if evect is tridiagonal). (Not referenced if evect is none).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n if evect is original or tridiagonal. Specifies the leading dimension of C. (Not referenced if evect is none).**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, STEQR did not converge. i elements of E did not converge to zero.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cstedc([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cstedc14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPfPfP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dstedc([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dstedc14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPdPdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sstedc([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sstedc14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK11rocblas_intPfPfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) STEDC computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a symmetric tridiagonal matrix.

This function uses the divide and conquer method to compute the eigenvectors. The eigenvalues are returned in increasing order.

The matrix is not represented explicitly, but rather as the array of diagonal elements D and the array of symmetric off-diagonal elements E. When D and E correspond to the tridiagonal form of a full symmetric/Hermitian matrix, as returned by, e.g.,

[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)or[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35), the eigenvectors of the original matrix can also be computed, depending on the value of evect.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies how the eigenvectors are computed.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the tridiagonal matrix.**D**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On entry, the diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**E**–**[inout]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. On entry, the off-diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix. On exit, if info = 0, the values of this array are destroyed.**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. On entry, if evect is original, the orthogonal/unitary matrix used for the reduction to tridiagonal form as returned by, e.g.,[ORGTR](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1acaa6f0e82b62cf3aee9522e09dcc421e)or[UNGTR](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a31b4297ed23d32e373c67858ab89fa23). On exit, if info = 0, it is overwritten with the eigenvectors of the original symmetric/Hermitian matrix (if evect is original), or the eigenvectors of the tridiagonal matrix (if evect is tridiagonal). (Not referenced if evect is none).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n if evect is original or tridiagonal. Specifies the leading dimension of C. (Not referenced if evect is none).**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, STEDC failed to compute an eigenvalue on the sub-matrix formed by the rows and columns info/(n+1) through mod(info,n+1).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zstein([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zstein14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdPdP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cstein([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cstein14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfPfP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dstein([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *D, double *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit, double *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dstein14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdPdP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sstein([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *D, float *E,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*iblock,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*isplit, float *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ifail,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sstein14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfPfP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) STEIN computes the eigenvectors associated with a set of provided eigenvalues of a symmetric tridiagonal matrix.

The eigenvectors of the symmetric tridiagonal matrix are computed using inverse iteration.

The matrix is not represented explicitly, but rather as the array of diagonal elements D and the array of symmetric off-diagonal elements E. The eigenvalues must be provided in the array W, as returned by

[STEBZ](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a947cefb6451b73cac1d62b609e9296f5).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the tridiagonal matrix.**D**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix.**E**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. The off-diagonal elements of the tridiagonal matrix.**nev**–**[in]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. 0 <= nev <= n. The number of provided eigenvalues, and the number of eigenvectors to be computed.**W**–**[in]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension >= nev. A subset of nev eigenvalues of the tridiagonal matrix, as returned by[STEBZ](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a947cefb6451b73cac1d62b609e9296f5).**iblock**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The block indices corresponding to each eigenvalue, as returned by[STEBZ](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a947cefb6451b73cac1d62b609e9296f5). If iblock[i] = k, then eigenvalue W[i] belongs to the k-th block from the top.**isplit**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The splitting indices that divide the tridiagonal matrix into diagonal blocks, as returned by[STEBZ](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a947cefb6451b73cac1d62b609e9296f5). The k-th block stretches from the end of the (k-1)-th block (or the top left corner of the tridiagonal matrix, in the case of the 1st block) to the isplit[k]-th row/column.**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev. On exit, contains the eigenvectors of the tridiagonal matrix corresponding to the provided eigenvalues, stored by columns.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of Z.**ifail**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. If info = 0, the first nev elements of ifail are zero. Otherwise, contains the indices of those eigenvectors that failed to converge.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, i eigenvectors did not converge; their indices are stored in IFAIL.



## Symmetric matrices[#](#symmetric-matrices)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zlasyf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*kb,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zlasyf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_clasyf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*kb,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_clasyf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dlasyf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*kb, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dlasyf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_slasyf([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*kb, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_slasyf14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) LASYF computes a partial factorization of a symmetric matrix \(A\) using Bunch-Kaufman diagonal pivoting.

The partial factorization has the form

\[\begin{split} A = \left[ \begin{array}{cc} I & U_{12} \\ 0 & U_{22} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{cc} A_{11} & 0 \\ 0 & D \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{cc} I & 0 \\ U_{12}^T & U_{22}^T \end{array} \right] \end{split}\]or

\[\begin{split} A = \left[ \begin{array}{cc} L_{11} & 0 \\ L_{21} & I \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{cc} D & 0 \\ 0 & A_{22} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{cc} L_{11}^T & L_{21}^T \\ 0 & I \end{array} \right] \end{split}\]depending on the value of uplo. The order of the block diagonal matrix \(D\) is either \(nb\) or \(nb-1\), and is returned in the argument \(kb\).

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 2 <= nb <= n. The number of columns of A to be factored.**kb**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The number of columns of A that were actually factored (either nb or nb-1).**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the symmetric matrix A to be factored. On exit, the partially factored matrix.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The vector of pivot indices. Elements of ipiv are 1-based indices. If uplo is upper, then only the last kb elements of ipiv will be set. For n - kb < k <= n, if ipiv[k] > 0 then rows and columns k and ipiv[k] were interchanged and D[k,k] is a 1-by-1 diagonal block. If, instead, ipiv[k] = ipiv[k-1] < 0, then rows and columns k-1 and -ipiv[k] were interchanged and D[k-1,k-1] to D[k,k] is a 2-by-2 diagonal block. If uplo is lower, then only the first kb elements of ipiv will be set. For 1 <= k <= kb, if ipiv[k] > 0 then rows and columns k and ipiv[k] were interchanged and D[k,k] is a 1-by-1 diagonal block. If, instead, ipiv[k] = ipiv[k+1] < 0, then rows and columns k+1 and -ipiv[k] were interchanged and D[k,k] to D[k+1,k+1] is a 2-by-2 diagonal block.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, D is singular. D[i,i] is the first diagonal zero.



## Orthonormal matrices[#](#orthonormal-matrices)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorg2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorg2r14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPd)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorg2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorg2r14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORG2R generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal columns.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k). \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= n <= m. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k columns. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorgqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorgqr14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPd)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorgqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorgqr14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORGQR generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal columns.

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:

The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k columns. [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorgl2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorgl214rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPd)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorgl2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorgl214rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORGL2 generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal rows.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first m rows of the product of k Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= m <= n. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= m. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k rows. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorglq([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorglq14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORGLQ generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal rows.

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first m rows of the product of k Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= m <= n. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= m. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k rows. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorg2l([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorg2l14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORG2L generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal columns.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the last n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= n <= m. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the last k columns. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the last n column of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorgbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorgbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORGBR generates an m-by-n Matrix Q with orthonormal rows or columns.

If storev is column-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal columns. If m >= k, Q is defined as the first n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]If m < k, Q is defined as the product of Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(m-1) \]On the other hand, if storev is row-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal rows. If n > k, Q is defined as the first m rows of the product of k Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]If n <= k, Q is defined as the product of Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(n-1)H(n-2)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8)in its arguments A and tauq or taup.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies whether to work column-wise or row-wise.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q. If row-wise, then min(n,k) <= m <= n.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix Q. If column-wise, then min(m,k) <= n <= m.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0. The number of columns (if storev is column-wise) or rows (if row-wise) of the original matrix reduced by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8). On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension min(m,k) if column-wise, or min(n,k) if row-wise. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorgtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorgtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPd)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorgtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorgtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPf) ORGTR generates an n-by-n orthogonal Matrix Q.

Q is defined as the product of n-1 Householder reflectors of order n. If uplo indicates upper, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(n-1)H(n-2)\cdots H(1) \]On the other hand, if uplo indicates lower, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(n-1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)in its arguments A and tau.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)factorization was upper or lower triangular. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix Q.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c). On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. The Householder scalars as returned by[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorm2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorm2r14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorm2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorm2r14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORM2R multiplies a matrix Q with orthonormal columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2) \cdots H(k) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QR factorization

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8)in the first k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, or lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dormqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dormqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sormqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sormqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORMQR multiplies a matrix Q with orthonormal columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QR factorization

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8)in the first k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, or lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dorml2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dorml214rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sorml2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sorml214rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORML2 multiplies a matrix Q with orthonormal rows by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the LQ factorization

[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*m if side is left, or lda*n if side is right. The Householder vectors as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6)in the first k rows of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= k. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dormql([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dormql14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)
