[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sormql([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sormql14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORMQL multiplies a matrix Q with orthonormal columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QL factorization

[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940)in the last k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dormbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dormbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sormbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sormbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORMBR multiplies a matrix Q with orthonormal rows or columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

If storev is column-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal columns. If storev is row-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal rows. The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]The order q of the orthogonal matrix Q is q = m if applying from the left, or q = n if applying from the right.

When storev is column-wise, if q >= k, then Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k), \]and if q < k, then Q is defined as the product

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1). \]When storev is row-wise, if q > k, then Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k), \]and if q <= k, Q is defined as the product

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1). \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors and scalars as returned by

[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8)in its arguments A and tauq or taup.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies whether to work column-wise or row-wise.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0. The number of columns (if storev is column-wise) or rows (if row-wise) of the original matrix reduced by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*min(q,k) if column-wise, or lda*q if row-wise. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= q if column-wise, or lda >= min(q,k) if row-wise. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least min(q,k). The Householder scalars as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dormtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dormtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK12rocblas_fillK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sormtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_sormtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK12rocblas_fillK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_int) ORMTR multiplies an orthogonal matrix Q by a general m-by-n matrix C.

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^TC & \: \text{Transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^T & \: \text{Transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]The order q of the orthogonal matrix Q is q = m if applying from the left, or q = n if applying from the right.

Q is defined as a product of q-1 Householder reflectors. If uplo indicates upper, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(q-1)H(q-2)\cdots H(1). \]On the other hand, if uplo indicates lower, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors and scalars as returned by

[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)in its arguments A and tau.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c)factorization was upper or lower triangular. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*q. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= q. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least q-1. The Householder scalars as returned by[SYTRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ad1fa528f53fe8c81cc85ffbd8874862c).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.



## Unitary matrices[#](#unitary-matrices)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zung2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zung2r14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complex)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cung2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cung2r14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex) UNG2R generates an m-by-n complex Matrix Q with orthonormal columns.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= n <= m. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k columns. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zungqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zungqr14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complex)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cungqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cungqr14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex) UNGQR generates an m-by-n complex Matrix Q with orthonormal columns.

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= n <= m. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= n. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k columns. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).



-

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cungl2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cungl214rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex) UNGL2 generates an m-by-n complex Matrix Q with orthonormal rows.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is defined as the first m rows of the product of k Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(k)^HH(k-1)^H\cdots H(1)^H \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= m <= n. The number of rows of the matrix Q.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix Q.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. 0 <= k <= m. The number of Householder reflectors.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8), with the Householder vectors in the first k rows. On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cungbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cungbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex) UNGBR generates an m-by-n complex Matrix Q with orthonormal rows or columns.

If storev is column-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal columns. If m >= k, Q is defined as the first n columns of the product of k Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]If m < k, Q is defined as the product of Householder reflectors of order m

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(m-1) \]On the other hand, if storev is row-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal rows. If n > k, Q is defined as the first m rows of the product of k Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]If n <= k, Q is defined as the product of Householder reflectors of order n

\[ Q = H(n-1)H(n-2)\cdots H(1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8)in its arguments A and tauq or taup.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies whether to work column-wise or row-wise.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix Q. If row-wise, then min(n,k) <= m <= n.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix Q. If column-wise, then min(m,k) <= n <= m.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0. The number of columns (if storev is column-wise) or rows (if row-wise) of the original matrix reduced by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8). On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension min(m,k) if column-wise, or min(n,k) if row-wise. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zungtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zungtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complex)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cungtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cungtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complex) UNGTR generates an n-by-n unitary Matrix Q.

Q is defined as the product of n-1 Householder reflectors of order n. If uplo indicates upper, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(n-1)H(n-2)\cdots H(1) \]On the other hand, if uplo indicates lower, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(n-1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors \(v_i\) and scalars \(\text{ipiv}[i]\), as returned by

[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35)in its arguments A and tau.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35)factorization was upper or lower triangular. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix Q.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35). On exit, the computed matrix Q.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n-1. The Householder scalars as returned by[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35).

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zunm2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zunm2r14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cunm2r([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cunm2r14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) UNM2R multiplies a complex matrix Q with orthonormal columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QR factorization

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8)in the first k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, or lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zunmqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zunmqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cunmqr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cunmqr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) UNMQR multiplies a complex matrix Q with orthonormal columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the blocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QR factorization

[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8)in the first k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, or lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a37b336b66ef8dd4d70e2ccff92f038d8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cunml2([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cunml214rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) UNML2 multiplies a complex matrix Q with orthonormal rows by a general m-by-n matrix C.

(This is the unblocked version of the algorithm).

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(k)^HH(k-1)^H\cdots H(1)^H \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the LQ factorization

[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*m if side is left, or lda*n if side is right. The Householder vectors as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6)in the first k rows of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= k. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GELQF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a99502a6fa094a310499dd853bc0db0d6).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(k)H(k-1)\cdots H(1) \]of order m if applying from the left, or n if applying from the right. Q is never stored, it is calculated from the Householder vectors and scalars returned by the QL factorization

[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0; k <= m if side is left, k <= n if side is right. The number of Householder reflectors that form Q.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*k. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940)in the last k columns of its argument A.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m if side is left, lda >= n if side is right. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least k. The Householder scalars as returned by[GEQLF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a740517e43f2216bc0555c2a719f02940).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zunmbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zunmbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cunmbr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_storev](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_storev)storev, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)k,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cunmbr14rocblas_handleK14rocblas_storevK12rocblas_sideK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) UNMBR multiplies a complex matrix Q with orthonormal rows or columns by a general m-by-n matrix C.

If storev is column-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal columns. If storev is row-wise, then the matrix Q has orthonormal rows. The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]The order q of the unitary matrix Q is q = m if applying from the left, or q = n if applying from the right.

When storev is column-wise, if q >= k, then Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k), \]and if q < k, then Q is defined as the product

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1). \]When storev is row-wise, if q > k, then Q is defined as the product of k Householder reflectors

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(k), \]and if q <= k, Q is defined as the product

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1). \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors and scalars as returned by

[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8)in its arguments A and tauq or taup.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**storev**–**[in]**[rocblas_storev](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1ad616d0ae9095fc1d87f14c7d1be0cff8). Specifies whether to work column-wise or row-wise.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**k**–**[in]**rocblas_int. k >= 0. The number of columns (if storev is column-wise) or rows (if row-wise) of the original matrix reduced by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*min(q,k) if column-wise, or lda*q if row-wise. The Householder vectors as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= q if column-wise, or lda >= min(q,k) if row-wise. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least min(q,k). The Householder scalars as returned by[GEBRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ab29f0ab4f03663b3179591fe072d42e8).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zunmtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zunmtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK12rocblas_fillK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cunmtr([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_side](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_side)side, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_operation](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv417rocblas_operation)trans, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*ipiv,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cunmtr14rocblas_handleK12rocblas_sideK12rocblas_fillK17rocblas_operationK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_int) UNMTR multiplies a unitary matrix Q by a general m-by-n matrix C.

The matrix Q is applied in one of the following forms, depending on the values of side and trans:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} QC & \: \text{No transpose from the left,}\\ Q^HC & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the left,}\\ CQ & \: \text{No transpose from the right, and}\\ CQ^H & \: \text{Conjugate transpose from the right.} \end{array} \end{split}\]The order q of the unitary matrix Q is q = m if applying from the left, or q = n if applying from the right.

Q is defined as a product of q-1 Householder reflectors. If uplo indicates upper, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(q-1)H(q-2)\cdots H(1). \]On the other hand, if uplo indicates lower, then Q has the form

\[ Q = H(1)H(2)\cdots H(q-1) \]The Householder matrices \(H(i)\) are never stored, they are computed from its corresponding Householder vectors and scalars as returned by

[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35)in its arguments A and tau.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**side**–**[in]**rocblas_side. Specifies from which side to apply Q.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35)factorization was upper or lower triangular. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**trans**–**[in]**rocblas_operation. Specifies whether the matrix Q or its conjugate transpose is to be applied.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. Number of rows of matrix C.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of columns of matrix C.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size lda*q. On entry, the Householder vectors as returned by[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= q. Leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension at least q-1. The Householder scalars as returned by[HETRD](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1abbf29fb7892cde18dc72ee4af83b2f35).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of size ldc*n. On entry, the matrix C. On exit, it is overwritten with Q*C, C*Q, Q’*C, or C*Q’.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= m. Leading dimension of C.
